    GetOrigin --> GetOriginLoc[location - origin]
    GetOriginLoc --> GetDest[actual_trip_stop - destination]

    PrintLegInfo --> LoopLegs
    LoopLegs --> CloseDBs[Close DB connections]

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class DatabaseConnections {
        +get_entity_db()
        +get_shipments_db()
        +db_query_dict()
    }
    class EntityOperations {
        +is_entity_delivered()
        +get_entity_delivery_date()
        +show_entity_info()
    }
    class TripLegOperations {
        +entity_planned_trip_legs()
        +entity_actual_trip_leg()
        +actual_trip_leg()
    }
    class LocationOperations {
        +actual_trip_stop()
        +location()
        +wrt_to_latlon()
    }
    class MainFlow {
        +main()
    }
    MainFlow --> DatabaseConnections
    MainFlow --> EntityOperations
    EntityOperations --> TripLegOperations
    TripLegOperations --> LocationOperations
    EntityOperations --> DatabaseConnections
    TripLegOperations --> DatabaseConnections
    LocationOperations --> DatabaseConnections
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Main
    participant ArgParser
    participant EntityDB
    participant ShipmentsDB
    participant ShowEntityInfo
    Main->>ArgParser: Parse entity_id
    ArgParser-->>Main: entity_id
    Main->>EntityDB: get_entity_db()
    EntityDB-->>Main: entity_db connection
    Main->>ShipmentsDB: get_shipments_db()
    ShipmentsDB-->>Main: shipments_db connection
    Main->>ShowEntityInfo: show_entity_info(entity_id)
    ShowEntityInfo->>EntityDB: Query entity by id
    EntityDB-->>ShowEntityInfo: entity_dict
    ShowEntityInfo->>ShowEntityInfo: is_entity_delivered()
    ShowEntityInfo->>ShowEntityInfo: get_entity_delivery_date()
    ShowEntityInfo->>EntityDB: entity_planned_trip_legs()
    EntityDB-->>ShowEntityInfo: planned legs list
    ShowEntityInfo->>EntityDB: entity_actual_trip_leg()
    EntityDB-->>ShowEntityInfo: actual legs list
    loop For each actual leg
        ShowEntityInfo->>EntityDB: actual_trip_leg(leg_id)
        EntityDB-->>ShowEntityInfo: leg details
        ShowEntityInfo->>EntityDB: actual_trip_stop(origin_id)
        EntityDB-->>ShowEntityInfo: origin stop
        ShowEntityInfo->>EntityDB: location(origin_location_id)
        EntityDB-->>ShowEntityInfo: origin location
        ShowEntityInfo->>EntityDB: actual_trip_stop(destination_id)
        EntityDB-->>ShowEntityInfo: destination stop
        ShowEntityInfo->>EntityDB: location(destination_location_id)
        EntityDB-->>ShowEntityInfo: destination location
    end
    ShowEntityInfo-->>Main: Complete
    Main->>EntityDB: Close connection
    Main->>ShipmentsDB: Close connection
```

## Diagram 5

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> NotDelivered
    NotDelivered --> InTransit: Entity created
    InTransit --> PlannedTrip: Trip legs planned
    PlannedTrip --> ActualTrip: Trip legs assigned
    ActualTrip --> InProgress: Entity in transit
    InProgress --> Delivered: state=delivered OR archived AND trip_plan_complete_source exists OR percentProgress=100
    Delivered --> [*]
```
